</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:12pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="height:42.75pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><span><br/></span></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:42.75pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span><br/></span></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:12pt"><span style="color:#5f0095;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:22pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Item&#160;2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On December&#160;16, 2021, Accenture plc (&#8220;Accenture&#8221;) issued a news release announcing financial results for its first quarter of fiscal 2022, which ended on November&#160;30, 2021.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A copy of the news release is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;99. All information in the news release is furnished but not filed.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:110%">Non-GAAP Financial Information</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the attached news release Accenture discloses the following non-GAAP financial measures:</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Free cash flow (defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions). Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this information provides meaningful additional information regarding the company&#8217;s liquidity.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Percentage changes in revenues and bookings on a local currency basis. Financial results in local currency are calculated by restating current period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior year period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates. This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Diluted earnings per share, effective tax rate, income before income taxes, income tax expense, and net income excluding gains on an investment. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding the effect of the investment gains facilitates an understanding as to the impacts of the investment and the company&#8217;s financial performance.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this non-GAAP financial information is useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:9pt"><span><br/></span></div><div excluding these gains, EPS are up 28% from adjusted EPS of $2.17 </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">in the first quarter last year -- </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">-- Operating income increases 29% to $2.43 billion, with operating margin of 16.3%, an </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">expansion of 20 basis points --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">-- New bookings are a record $16.8&#160;billion, a 30% increase in both U.S. dollars and local </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">currency from the first quarter last year, with record consulting bookings of $9.4&#160;billion and outsourcing bookings of $7.4&#160;billion --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">-- Company declares quarterly cash dividend of $0.97 per share, up 10% from a year ago --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">-- Accenture raises its business outlook for fiscal 2022&#59; now expects full-year revenue growth of 19% to 22% in local currency&#59; EPS of $10.32 to $10.60&#59; and free cash flow of $7.7&#160;billion to $8.2&#160;billion --   <br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">NEW YORK&#59; Dec. 16, 2021 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE&#58; ACN) reported financial results for the first quarter of fiscal 2022, ended Nov. 30, 2021, with revenues of $15.0&#160;billion, an increase of 27% in both U.S. dollars and local currency over the same period last year. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Diluted earnings per share were $2.78, a 20% increase from $2.32 for the first quarter last year, which included $0.15 in gains on an investment. On an adjusted basis, EPS increased 28% from $2.17 for the first quarter last year.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Operating income was $2.43 billion, a 29% increase over the same period last year, and operating margin was 16.3%, an expansion of 20 basis points.    </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">New bookings for the quarter were a record $16.8 billion, with record consulting bookings of $9.4&#160;billion and outsourcing bookings of $7.4 billion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Julie Sweet, Accenture&#8217;s Chair &#38; CEO, said, &#8220;We were pleased to continue delivering 360&#176; value for our clients as they accelerate their digital transformations. Our outstanding first-quarter financial performance and ability to capitalize on the market opportunity reflects continued market share gains. This is the direct result of having executed for years a strategy to rotate our business to digital, cloud and security, both hiring and upskilling exceptionally talented people across the globe and fostering deep relationships with both the world&#8217;s leading companies and our technology partners. I am especially proud that we added 50,000 people to our workforce this quarter, now at 674,000, reflecting our strong employee experience, which enables us to attract and grow great people.&#8221;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#160;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#8220;Our goal is to create 360&#176; value for all our stakeholders and reflects our growth strategy, our core values and our culture of shared success &#8212; succeeding not only financially, but in dimensions of value such as inclusion and diversity, reskilling, sustainability and experience. And today, we are launching our integrated 360&#176; Value Reporting Experience, a new way to share the value we create in all directions.&#8221;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline"><br></font></div><div style="height:18pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Financial Review</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Revenues for the first quarter of fiscal 2022 were $14.97&#160;billion, compared with $11.76&#160;billion for the first quarter of fiscal 2021, an increase of 27% in both U.S. dollars and local currency. Revenues were more than $600 million above the company&#8217;s guided range of $13.90 billion to $14.35 billion. The foreign-exchange impact for the quarter was approximately flat, compared with the assumption of a positive 0.5% impact provided in the company&#8217;s fourth-quarter earnings release. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;padding-left:14.11pt">Consulting revenues for the quarter were $8.39 billion, an increase of 33% in U.S. dollars and 32% in local currency compared with the first quarter of fiscal 2021. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;padding-left:14.11pt">Outsourcing revenues were $6.57&#160;billion, an increase of 21% in both U.S. dollars and local currency compared with the first quarter of fiscal 2021. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Diluted EPS for the quarter were $2.78, a 20% increase from $2.32 for the first quarter last year, which included pre-tax gains on an investment of $120 million, or $0.15 per share. Excluding these gains, EPS increased 28% from adjusted EPS of $2.17 for the first quarter of fiscal 2021. The $0.61 increase in EPS on an adjusted basis reflects&#58;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.64&#160;increase from higher revenue and operating results&#59; and </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01 increase from a lower share count&#59;   </font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">partially offset by</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.03 decrease from a higher effective tax rate&#59; and  </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01 decrease from higher income attributable to noncontrolling interests.    </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the quarter was 32.9%, compared with 33.1% for the first quarter last year. Selling, general and administrative (SG&#38;A) expenses for the quarter were $2.48&#160;billion, or 16.6% of revenues, compared with $2.01&#160;billion, or 17.1% of revenues, for the first quarter last year.     </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Operating income for the quarter increased 29%, to $2.43 billion, or 16.3% of revenues, compared with $1.89 billion, or 16.1% of revenues, for the first quarter of fiscal 2021.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">The company&#8217;s effective tax rate for the quarter was 24.4%, compared with 23.4% for the first quarter last year. Excluding the investment gains and the related tax expense of $23 million, the effective tax rate for the first quarter of fiscal 2021 was 23.7%. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Net income for the quarter was $1.82 billion, compared with $1.52 billion for the first quarter last year. Excluding after-tax investment gains of $97 million, net income for the first quarter of fiscal 2021 was $1.43 billion.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Operating cash flow for the quarter was $531 million, and property and equipment additions were $182&#160;million. Free cash flow, defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions, was $349 million. For the same period last year, operating cash flow was $1.60&#160;billion&#59; property and equipment additions were $93&#160;million&#59; and free cash flow was $1.51&#160;billion.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:18pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Days services outstanding, or DSOs, were 42 days at Nov. 30, 2021, compared with 38 days at Aug. 31, 2021 and 38 days at Nov. 30, 2020. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Accenture&#8217;s total cash balance at Nov. 30, 2021 was $5.6&#160;billion, compared with $8.2&#160;billion at Aug. 31, 2021.  </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%"><br>New Bookings</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New bookings for the first quarter were a record $16.8&#160;billion, a 30% increase in both U.S. dollars and local currency from the first quarter last year.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div bookings.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font bookings.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Revenues by Geographic Market</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues by geographic market were as follows&#58; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Products&#58; $4.28&#160;billion, an increase of 34% in both U.S. dollars and local currency compared with the first quarter of fiscal 2021.   </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Resources&#58; $1.95&#160;billion, an increase of 17% in both U.S. dollars and local currency compared with the first quarter of fiscal 2021.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Returning Cash to Shareholders</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture continues to return cash to shareholders through cash dividends and share repurchases.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:18pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Dividend</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On Nov. 15, 2021, a quarterly cash dividend of $0.97 per share was paid to shareholders of record at the close of business on Oct. 14, 2021. These cash dividend payments totaled $613&#160;million.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture plc has declared another quarterly cash dividend of $0.97 per share for shareholders of record at the close of business on Jan. 13, 2022. This dividend, which is payable on Feb. 15, 2022, represents a 10% increase over the quarterly dividend rate of $0.88 per share in fiscal 2021.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Share Repurchase Activity</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">During the first quarter of fiscal 2022, Accenture repurchased or redeemed 2.4&#160;million shares for a total of $845 million, including approximately 1.9 million shares repurchased in the open market.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture&#8217;s total remaining share repurchase authority at Nov. 30, 2021 was approximately $5.6&#160;billion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">At Nov. 30, 2021, Accenture had approximately 633&#160;million total shares outstanding.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Business Outlook</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Second Quarter Fiscal 2022</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Accenture expects revenues for the second quarter of fiscal 2022 to be in the range of $14.30&#160;billion to $14.75&#160;billion, an increase of 22% to 26% in local currency, reflecting the company&#8217;s assumption of a negative 4% foreign-exchange impact compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2021.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Fiscal Year 2022</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">&#160;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Accenture&#8217;s business outlook for the full 2022 fiscal year now assumes that the foreign-exchange impact on its results in U.S. dollars will be approximately negative 3% compared with fiscal 2021&#59; the company previously expected a negative 0.5% foreign-exchange impact. &#160;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">For fiscal 2022, the company now expects revenue growth to be in the range of 19% to 22% in local currency, compared with 12% to 15% previously. </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#160;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Accenture continues to expect operating margin for the full fiscal year to be in the range of 15.2% to 15.4%, an expansion of 10 to 30 basis points from fiscal 2021. </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#160;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The company continues to expect its annual effective tax rate to be in the range of 23.0% to 25.0%.&#160; </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#160;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The company now expects GAAP diluted EPS to be in the range of $10.32 to $10.60, compared with $9.90 to $10.18 previously, an increase of 17% to 20% over adjusted FY21 diluted EPS of $8.80 &#8212; which exclude gains on an investment of $0.36 from FY21 GAAP diluted EPS of $9.16. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:18pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div 2022, the company now expects operating cash flow to be in the range of $8.4 billion to $8.9 billion, compared with $8.2&#160;billion to $8.7&#160;billion previously&#59; continues to expect property and equipment additions to be $700&#160;million&#59; and now expects free cash flow to be in the range of $7.7 billion to $8.2 billion, compared with $7.5&#160;billion to $8.0&#160;billion previously.&#160; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The company continues to
